name:c‚Äçb‚Äçt‚Äçg‚Äç-‚Äç5‚Äç5‚Äç2‚Äç2

posted:Posted November 22, 2023
msg:Hilton Urumqi gave me a very pleasant stay. The hotel is located in the convention and exhibition area, with the Xinjiang International Convention and Exhibition Center to the east and the entrance to the Hongguang Mountain Scenic Area to the west. There are several commercial complexes such as Greentown and Wuyue nearby. The hotel is located at the southern foot of Hongguang Mountain. It covers a large area and has sufficient space to create a garden-style parking lot. The shape of the building is like rolling hills and undulating sea water.
Rows of chandeliers of different lengths create a sense of rhythm in the lobby on the first floor. The lobby bar and cafeteria are both on this floor. The front desk helped to upgrade to an executive room and provided executive lounge privileges. It is really good to have such service on weekends when there are a lot of people. The room is located on the 11th floor, which is the top floor of the hotel. The light wooden furniture and the lake blue patterned carpet make the room both elegant and warm. The hotel has sufficient heating, so you don't need to wear any thick clothes in the room. The toiletries are from Crabtree and have green apple scent. The bathing space is surrounded by the bathroom corridor and the room corridor to form a "room within a room". The room overlooks the Hongguang Mountain Buddhist Temple and a lake at the northern foot.
The happy hour buffet in the executive lounge solved my dinner dilemma. The product and quantity were just right, and it was also equipped with an all-in-one printing and copying machine for office use. The buffet breakfast is very rich, combining Chinese and Western styles for you to choose from. The dining environment is also very comfortable, maybe because there are fewer people during the off-season.
The swimming pool is located on the third floor. From the elevator to the entrance, you have to walk down a long corridor. On the way, you pass by the periphery of a Chinese restaurant and teahouse, as well as a calligraphy and painting exhibition. The swimming pool has ample space, clear water, suitable water temperature, the wall lights are on, and there is a hot and cold massage pool next to it. It is so comfortable to encounter such a swimming pool in Urumqi, which is about to enter winter. The only flaw is that the mosaics on the pool wall and bottom have fallen off and were not repaired in time. The edges of some of the paving stones on the pool bank are very sharp, which can easily cause safety hazards.
